	PlaySE(4, "ps3/s14/06/220600006", 256, 64);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「沙都子はどうです？」",
			NULL, "\"How is Satoko?\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//入江rvS14/10/22100147.「大丈夫です。kvS14/10/22100148.薬が効いてよく眠っていますが…心配ありませんよ」
	PlaySE(4, "ps3/s14/10/22100147", 256, 64);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「大丈夫です。",
			NULL, "\"She's doing all right.", Line_WaitForInput);
	PlaySE(4, "ps3/s14/10/22100148", 256, 64);
	OutputLine(NULL, "薬が効いてよく眠っていますが…心配ありませんよ」",
			NULL, " She's sleeping well thanks to the medicine... so there's nothing to worry about.\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DrawBustshot( 4, "sprite/normal/si1a_huteki_a1_0", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 19, 200, TRUE );

//詩音rvS14/06/220600007.「――なら、好都合ですね」
	PlaySE(4, "ps3/s14/06/220600007", 256, 64);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「——なら、好都合ですね」",
			NULL, "\"...Then, that's convenient.\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	FadeOutBGM(2, 200, FALSE);
	PlaySE(3, "mc071", 256, 64);
	DrawScene("white", 250 );
	DrawScene("black", 500 );

//入江rvS14/10/22100149.「――え？！」
	PlaySE(4, "ps3/s14/10/22100149", 256, 64);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「——え？！」",
			NULL, "\"...Huh?!\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//r背後で火薬がはじけるような音が聞こえ、目の前の薬棚が、派手な音を立てて砕け散るのが見える。
	OutputLine(NULL, "背後で火薬がはじけるような音が聞こえ、目の前の薬棚が、派手な音を立てて砕け散るのが見える。",
			NULL, "I heard a sound like bursting gunpowder coming from behind, as the medicine rack in front of me shattered with a flashy sound.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//r驚いて振り返ると詩音は、冷え冷えとした視線を向けて、…ぬいぐるみの中に隠していたのか拳銃を構え立っていた。
	OutputLine(NULL, "驚いて振り返ると詩音は、冷え冷えとした視線を向けて、…ぬいぐるみの中に隠していたのか拳銃を構え立っていた。",
			NULL, "When I turned around in a panic, I found Shion coldly glaring this way... standing there holding a pistol that she must've been hiding inside the stuffed animal.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DrawBustshot( 4, "sprite/normal/si1a_hig_majime_a1_0", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 19, 200, FALSE );
	DrawScene("background/sinryou_sinsatu1", 1000 );

//詩音rvS14/06/220600008.「あなたに…聞きたいことがあります」
	PlaySE(4, "ps3/s14/06/220600008", 256, 64);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「あなたに…聞きたいことがあります」",
			NULL, "\"You... There's something I need to ask you.\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DrawBustshot( 4, "sprite/normal/si1a_hig_ikari_a1_0", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 19, 200, TRUE );

//詩音rvS14/06/220600009.「悟史くんは――どこ？」
	PlaySE(4, "ps3/s14/06/220600009", 256, 64);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「悟史くんは——どこ？」",
			NULL, "\"Where... is Satoshi-kun?\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DisableWindow();
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 3000 );
	DrawBustshotWithFiltering(6, "cinema", "x", 1, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 1300, TRUE );
	DrawBustshot(7, "title02", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 26, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 2000 );
	DrawBustshot(6, "black", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	FadeBustshotWithFiltering( 7, "x", 1, FALSE, 0, 0, 1000, TRUE );
	DrawScene( "black", 3000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

}
